    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 5000 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet=800
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END
Uorder=3
 TEMP order=3

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet=800
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END
Uorder=3
 TEMP order=3

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet=800
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

            DEFINES     REGION/     DEPENDS                      BASE          CSE
 EQUATION     VAR    COMPARTMENT      VAR         FUNCTION     COMPLEXITY   COMPLEXITY     MEMORY  DEFINITION
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PRIMARY EQUATIONS
     1       TEMP                            Field Equation                                      : (DT((TEMP*RHO)*CP))-(QVOL-(DIV(QDOT)))
                           1                         Source          9           10          800 : <Vb>(25/(( 0.40000*Vintegral#3)+( 0.39000*Vintegral#4)))
                                             Space Galerkin         18            9          720 : (<Vb>.Y( 0.50000*TEMP.Y))+(<Vb>.X( 0.50000*TEMP.X))
                                              Time Galerkin          0            4          320 : <Vb>(TEMP.T* 1.75e+6)
                                     TEMP    Space Jacobian         18            9          720 : (<Vb>.Y( 0.50000*Beta.Y))+(<Vb>.X( 0.50000*Beta.X))
                                     TEMP     Time Jacobian          0            6          480 : <Vb>((Beta*/Dt)* 1.75e+6)
                                           Surface Galerkin         10           10          800 : -((<S>.Y( 0.50000*TEMP.Y))+(<S>.X( 0.50000*TEMP.X)))
                                     TEMP  Surface Jacobian         10           10          800 : -((<S>.Y( 0.50000*Beta.Y))+(<S>.X( 0.50000*Beta.X)))
                           2                         Source          9           10          800 : <Vb>(200/(( 0.40000*Vintegral#3)+( 0.39000*Vintegral#4)))
                                             Space Galerkin         10            5          400 : (<Vb>.Y(TEMP.Y))+(<Vb>.X(TEMP.X))
                                              Time Galerkin          0            4          320 : <Vb>(TEMP.T* 5.04e+6)

   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet=800
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100|

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

                                              Time Galerkin          0            4          320 : <Vb>(TEMP.T* 1.75e+6)
                                     TEMP    Space Jacobian         18            9          720 : (<Vb>.Y( 0.50000*Beta.Y))+(<Vb>.X( 0.50000*Beta.X))

    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet=800
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END

SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS

In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet=800
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet= 400
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet= 400
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS
==========================
In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

    1| TITLE 'New Problem'     { the problem identification }
    2| 
    3| COORDINATES cartesian2  { coordinate system, 1D,2D,3D, etc }
    4| 
    5| VARIABLES        { system variables }
    6| 
    7| Temp(threshold=.01) !temperature in degC
    8| 
    9| DEFINITIONS    { parameter definitions }
   10| 
   11| !Variables Params
   12| T_air = 100 !Degrees celcius
   13| h = 100 !The convection heat transfer coefficient
   14| Power_mic = 500 !The power of the microwave W
   15| 
   16| rho
   17| k
   18| cp
   19| epsilon_m
   20| T_Ideal
   21| initTemp
   22| 
   23| rho_filling=1200 !kg/m^3
   24| rho_crust=700 !kg/m^3
   25| area_filling=1/2*pi*0.035^2 !m^3
   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet= 400
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }
  102| 
  103| PLOTS            { save result displays }
  104| for t = 0 by endtime/5 to endtime
  105|   CONTOUR(Temp) painted
  106|  !vector(qdot) norm
  107| SUMMARY
  108| report(tastiness)
  109| 
  110| 
  111| END

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS

In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.

   26| area_crust=(0.005*0.08+1/2*pi*0.04^2-1/2*pi*0.035^2)
   27| Ttol=4
   28| massf=rho_filling*area_filling*.39 !filling mass
   29| massc=rho_crust*area_crust*.4 !crust mass
   30| mass=massf+massc
   31| T_integral=.4*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'crust')+0.39*area_integral(rho*((Temp-T_ideal)/Ttol)^4, 'filling')
   32| Tastiness=1/(1+T_integral/mass)
   33| !Skillet values
   34| 
   35| k_skillet = 10 !W/m^2-K
   36| rho_skillet = 3500 !kg/m^3
   37| cp_skillet = 1300 !J/kg-K
   38| thickness_skillet = 0.005 !m thick
   39| width_skillet = 0.09 !m wide
   40| length_skillet = 0.41 !m long
   41| Power_skillet= 400
   42|  !Volumetric Heating in the Skillet
   43| 
   44| absorb_tot =  0.4*area_integral(epsilon_m,'crust') + 0.39*(area_integral(epsilon_m, "filling"))
   45| 
   46| radius_crust = 0.04 !radius of the crust in meters
   47| radius_filling = 0.035
   48| qvol
   49| qdot = -k*grad(Temp)
   50| INITIAL VALUES
   51| Temp =inittemp
   52|     
   53| EQUATIONS        { PDE's, one for each variable }
   54| 
   55|  dt(temp*rho*cp)=qvol- div(qdot)
   56| 
   57| 
   58| ! CONSTRAINTS    { Integral constraints }
   59| 
   60| BOUNDARIES       { The domain definition }
   61| 
   62|  REGION 'crust'       { For each material region }
   63|   !Crust values
   64|   	k = 0.5 !W/m^2-K
   65| 	rho = 700 !kg/m^3
   66| 	cp = 2500 !J/kg-K
   67| 	epsilon_m = 0.05 !Percent * 0.01
   68| 	T_ideal= 75 !Degrees celcius
   69|   	inittemp=4
   70| 	qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   71|     
   72| 	START(radius_crust,0)  load(temp)=h*(temp-t_air) { Walk the domain boundary }
   73| 		line to (radius_crust,0.005) arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 
   74| 		line to (-radius_crust,0)  line to (0,0) line to (radius_crust,0) to close
   75| 
   76| 	
   77|     REGION 'filling'
   78|         k = 1 !W/m^2-K
   79| 		rho = 1200 !kg/m^3
   80| 		epsilon_m = 0.4 ! Percent + 0.01
   81|         cp = 4200 ! J/kg-K
   82| 		T_ideal = 75 !Degrees celcius
   83| 		initTemp=4
   84| 		
   85| 		qvol=(Power_mic*epsilon_m)/absorb_tot
   86| 		start(radius_filling,0.005) !value(temp)=0
   87| 			arc(center=0,0.005) angle 180 load(temp) = 0 
   88| 			line to (0,0.005) to close
   89| 	REGION 'skillet'
   90| 	k = 10 !W/m^2-K
   91| 	rho = 3500 !kg/m^3
   92| 	cp = 1300 !J/kg-K
   93| 	epsilon_m=0
   94| 	initTemp=24
   95| 	T_ideal=0
   96| 	qvol = Power_Skillet/(thickness_skillet*(width_skillet*length_skillet/2+width_skillet/2*length_skillet/2))
   97| 	start   (width_skillet/2,0) load(temp)=0 line to (width_skillet/2,-thickness_skillet) 
   98| 	line to  (-width_skillet/2, -thickness_skillet) line to  (-width_skillet/2,0)  
   99| 	line to (0,0) to close
  100| 
  101| TIME 0 TO  60{ if time dependent }

  108| report(tastiness)

==========================
SUMMARIZE EQUATIONS

In the following equation definitions
Derivatives are represented by appending a dot and the differentiated coordinate.
The operator <V> represents volume integration. <Vb> is weighted by basis function.
<Vu> is weighted by the upwind modifer. <Vbu> is weighted by both.
A dotted volume integral represents volume integration weighted by the indicated
derivative of the basis function. 'Beta' represents a basis function.
The operator <S>.c represents surface integration weighted by the indicated
direction cosine.
